<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переключиться.html>переключи́ться</a> (14103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключить.html>переключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключиться.html>переключи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereključítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключаться.html>переключа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to switch, to switch over</li>
<li>to switch over <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:французский.html>францу́зский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затем.html>зате́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переключиться.html>переключи́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on učíl francúzskij jazýk, a zatém <b>pereključílsja</b> na anglíjskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he learned French, but then switched over to English</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переключиться.html>переключи́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:производство.html>произво́дство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:велосипед.html>велосипе́дов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zavód <b>pereključílsja</b> na proizvódstvo velosipédov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the factory switched over to the production of bicycles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переключить.html>переключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перекосить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекосить.html>перекоси́ть</a> (9915)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косить.html>коси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kosítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mow, to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекосить.html>перекоси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перека́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mow (the whole part of something)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mow down, to kill</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косить.html>коси́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скосить.html>скоси́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">косе́ц</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">koséc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косилка.html>коси́лка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kosílka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косить.html>коси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kosítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to twist, to slant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекосить.html>перекоси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перека́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доска.html>доску</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:рама.html>ра́му</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекосить.html>перекоси́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dosku (rámu) <b>perekosílo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the board (frame) has warped</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(face with anger, pain etc)</i> to twist, to contort, to distort
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекосить.html>перекоси́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекосить.html>перекоси́ло</a></b>) <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>perekosílo</b> licó (jevó <b>perekosílo</b>) ot boli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his face was twisted/distorted in pain; his face contorted with pain</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекосить.html>перекоси́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнев.html>гне́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>perekosílo</b> ot gnéva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his face contorted with rage</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***перекрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a> (11955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exceed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рекорд.html>реко́рд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> rekórd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break a record</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stop up, to block
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:русло.html>ру́сло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реки́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:плотина.html>плоти́ной</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekryvátʹ</b> rúslo rekí (plotínoj)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dam a river</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekryvátʹ</b> dorógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to block the roads; set up roadblocks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekryvátʹ</b> úlicu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to block (cordon off) the street</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отступление.html>отступле́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekryvátʹ</b> komú-libo putí k otstupléniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut off someone's escape/retreat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekryvátʹ</b> vódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut off the water</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кислород.html>кислоро́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perekryvátʹ kisloród</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a lid on, put the kibosh on</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overlap</li>
<li>to re-cover
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekryvátʹ</b> krýšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a new roof</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trump, to overtrump</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекрытие.html>перекры́тие</a> (15918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрытие.html>перекры́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekrýtije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрытие.html>перекры́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрытие.html>перекры́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрытие.html>перекры́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> floor, ceiling, overhead cover</li>

<li>blocking, damming</li></ol>

***перекрыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a> (7898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekrýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрывать.html>перекрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exceed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рекорд.html>реко́рд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> rekórd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break a record</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stop up, to block
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:русло.html>ру́сло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реки́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:плотина.html>плоти́ной</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> rúslo rekí (plotínoj)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dam a river</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> dorógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to block the roads; set up roadblocks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> úlicu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to block (cordon off) the street</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отступление.html>отступле́нию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> komú-libo putí k otstupléniju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut off someone's escape/retreat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> vódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut off the water</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кислород.html>кислоро́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perekrýtʹ kisloród</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a lid on, put the kibosh on</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overlap</li>
<li>to re-cover
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перекрыть.html>перекры́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perekrýtʹ</b> krýšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a new roof</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trump, to overtrump</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекурить.html>перекури́ть</a> (20386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перекурить.html>перекури́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perekurítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переку́ривать</b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smoke (all or many kinds of something)</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel bad or damage one's health from smoking too much</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take a smoking break</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">куси́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перелет.html>перелёт</a> (9725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелет.html>перелёт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereljót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелет.html>перелёта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелет.html>перелёты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелет.html>перелётов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(of birds)</i> transmigration</li>
<li><i>(of an airplane)</i> flight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">беспосадочный <a href = vnd.unilang:перелет.html>перелёт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">besposadočnyj pereljót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nonstop flight</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>shot over the target</li></ol>

***перелетавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перелетать.html>перелета́вший</a> (23162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***перелетать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перелетать.html>перелета́ть</a> (23162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелетать.html>перелета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелететь.html>перелете́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(from one place to another or above something)</i></li>
<li>to fly too far, to overshoot <i>(the mark)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***перелететь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перелететь.html>перелете́ть</a> (13141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелететь.html>перелете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereletétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелетать.html>перелета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly <i>(from one place to another or above something)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́ца</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перелететь.html>перелете́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одного́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:куст.html>куста́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ptíca <b>pereletéla</b> s odnovó kustá na drugój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the bird flew from one bush to another</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">самолёт <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перелететь.html>перелете́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:океан.html>океа́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">samoljót <b>pereletél</b> okeán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the plane flew across the ocean</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перелететь.html>перелете́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сетка.html>се́тку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjač ne <b>pereletél</b> čerez sétku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the ball didn't make it over the net</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fly too far, to overshoot <i>(the mark)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелет.html>перелёт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pereljót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перелетный.html>перелётный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pereljótnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
